msg:When I came to Xiongan in the cold winter, I chose Wyndham Hotel Xiongan. When design is integrated into architecture, when art is integrated into leisure, visual impact and ideological awakening will always bring about more exciting collisions. I heard from the hotel staff that the lobby is nine meters high and has local culture. The history is integrated into the space, allowing history and contemporary art to blend together. The young man who received the reception was very handsome and enthusiastic. When I entered the room, it was really amazing. The room I stayed in was the best to watch the sunset. From the thoughtful and convenient room facilities, 55-inch high-definition LCD TV, AI smart butler, Philips air purifier and other high-end facilities, every detail was given. The warmth of the guests made me feel the hotel's meticulous attention to detail, and the experience was unparalleled. For those who love to eat, food is the most important thing. There is nothing better than savoring the local specialties and allowing your taste buds to have an unexpected encounter. The Elements all-day dining restaurant offers a rich variety of Chinese and Western buffet breakfasts and local specialties. It provides borderless cuisine and creative delicacies with local characteristics, as well as delicious seafood. Eating, drinking and having fun are elegant, and the color, fragrance and taste are unique. I was deeply impressed by Ellie at the hotel. She provided full service from the moment we entered the hotel. I would like to thank her for upgrading our room for free. She also personally delivered fruit to the room. She was worried that we would be tired from the journey and even offered a footbath bucket. It was touching and heart-warming. Finally After leaving the hotel, they also helped me mail the items I left behind. Thanks to Ellie's meticulous and considerate service during this trip, I had a perfect stay!
